this interval function determines and, if necessary, returns the minimum/lower and maximum/upper interval limits of the absolute value function (e.\+g. abs(x)) with the specified precision 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em handle\+\_\+e\+Operator\+\_\+in} & specifies identifies the type of operator (e.\+g. ADDITION\+\_\+\+SIGN) for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em use\+Calculation\+Precision\+\_\+in} & specifies the precision for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em result\+\_\+in} & specifies the result of the standard calculation, i.\+e. without interval arithmetic \\
\hline
{\em error\+\_\+out} & the buffer whether an error occurred during the individual calculation (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em handle\+\_\+content\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the first operand for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies whether the first operand is an interval value \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Min\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the minimum/lower interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum/upper interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Min\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the minimum/lower interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the maximum/upper interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves whether the result of the individual calculation is an interval value (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em number\+Of\+Trusted\+Digits\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum precision in digits for this individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em reference\+Pecision\+Cut\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum number of digits that are not trusted for this individual calculation \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\hline
{\em number\+Of\+Trusted\+Digits\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum precision in digits for this individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em reference\+Pecision\+Cut\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum number of digits that are not trusted for this individual calculation \\

this interval function determines and, if necessary, returns the minimum/lower and maximum/upper interval limits of the cosine function (e.\+g. cos(x)) with the specified precision 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em handle\+\_\+e\+Operator\+\_\+in} & specifies identifies the type of operator (e.\+g. ADDITION\+\_\+\+SIGN) for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em use\+Calculation\+Precision\+\_\+in} & specifies the precision for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em result\+\_\+in} & specifies the result of the standard calculation, i.\+e. without interval arithmetic \\
\hline
{\em error\+\_\+out} & the buffer whether an error occurred during the individual calculation (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em handle\+\_\+content\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the first operand for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies whether the first operand is an interval value \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Min\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the minimum/lower interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum/upper interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Min\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the minimum/lower interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the maximum/upper interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves whether the result of the individual calculation is an interval value (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em number\+Of\+Trusted\+Digits\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum precision in digits for this individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em reference\+Pecision\+Cut\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum number of digits that are not trusted for this individual calculation \\
\hline

{\em handle\+\_\+e\+Operator\+\_\+in} & specifies identifies the type of operator (e.\+g. ADDITION\+\_\+\+SIGN) for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em use\+Calculation\+Precision\+\_\+in} & specifies the precision for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em result\+\_\+in} & specifies the result of the standard calculation, i.\+e. without interval arithmetic \\
\hline
{\em error\+\_\+out} & the buffer whether an error occurred during the individual calculation (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em handle\+\_\+content\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the first operand for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies whether the first operand is an interval value \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Min\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the minimum/lower interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum/upper interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Min\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the minimum/lower interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the maximum/upper interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves whether the result of the individual calculation is an interval value (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em number\+Of\+Trusted\+Digits\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum precision in digits for this individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em reference\+Pecision\+Cut\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum number of digits that are not trusted for this individual calculation \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

this interval function determines and, if necessary, returns the minimum/lower and maximum/upper interval limits of whether a floating point number is greater than 0 (1) or not greater than 0 (0), with the specified precision (e.\+g. "{}ispos(x)"{}) 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em handle\+\_\+e\+Operator\+\_\+in} & specifies identifies the type of operator (e.\+g. ADDITION\+\_\+\+SIGN) for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em use\+Calculation\+Precision\+\_\+in} & specifies the precision for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em result\+\_\+in} & specifies the result of the standard calculation, i.\+e. without interval arithmetic \\
\hline
{\em error\+\_\+out} & the buffer whether an error occurred during the individual calculation (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em handle\+\_\+content\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the first operand for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies whether the first operand is an interval value \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Min\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the minimum/lower interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum/upper interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Min\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the minimum/lower interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the maximum/upper interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves whether the result of the individual calculation is an interval value (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em number\+Of\+Trusted\+Digits\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum precision in digits for this individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em reference\+Pecision\+Cut\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum number of digits that are not trusted for this individual calculation \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

this interval function determines and, if necessary, returns the minimum/lower and maximum/upper interval limits of the hyperbolic tangent function (e.\+g. tanh(x)) with the specified precision 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em handle\+\_\+e\+Operator\+\_\+in} & specifies identifies the type of operator (e.\+g. ADDITION\+\_\+\+SIGN) for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em use\+Calculation\+Precision\+\_\+in} & specifies the precision for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em result\+\_\+in} & specifies the result of the standard calculation, i.\+e. without interval arithmetic \\
\hline
{\em error\+\_\+out} & the buffer whether an error occurred during the individual calculation (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em handle\+\_\+content\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the first operand for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies whether the first operand is an interval value \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Min\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the minimum/lower interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum/upper interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Min\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the minimum/lower interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the maximum/upper interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves whether the result of the individual calculation is an interval value (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em number\+Of\+Trusted\+Digits\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum precision in digits for this individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em reference\+Pecision\+Cut\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum number of digits that are not trusted for this individual calculation \\
\hline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool paceval\+\_\+handle\+Interval\+\_\+\+LESS\+\_\+\+THAN\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+OR\+\_\+\+ZERO\+\_\+\+FUNCTION (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{paceval__c_common_data_8h_ad9735d0e77b3ab4d3f71e690c5832670}{paceval\+\_\+e\+Operator\+Types}}}]{handle\+\_\+e\+Operator\+\_\+in,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{paceval__main_8h_af9beba80b657f547c9610aa0bb40e11e}{paceval\+\_\+e\+Calculation\+Precision\+Types}}}]{use\+Calculation\+Precision\+\_\+in,  }\item[{const long double \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{result\+\_\+in,  }\item[{bool \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{error\+\_\+out,  }\item[{const void \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{handle\+\_\+content\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in,  }\item[{bool \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{stack\+Of\+Has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in,  }\item[{const long double \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Min\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in,  }\item[{const long double \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in,  }\item[{long double \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{trusted\+Min\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out,  }\item[{long double \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{trusted\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out,  }\item[{bool \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out,  }\item[{const int}]{number\+Of\+Trusted\+Digits\+\_\+in,  }\item[{const int}]{reference\+Pecision\+Cut\+\_\+in }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

this interval function determines and, if necessary, returns the minimum/lower and maximum/upper interval limits of whether a floating point number is less than 0 or 0 (1) or not less than 0 or not 0 (0), with the specified precision (e.\+g. "{}isnegq(x)"{}) 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em handle\+\_\+e\+Operator\+\_\+in} & specifies identifies the type of operator (e.\+g. ADDITION\+\_\+\+SIGN) for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em use\+Calculation\+Precision\+\_\+in} & specifies the precision for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em result\+\_\+in} & specifies the result of the standard calculation, i.\+e. without interval arithmetic \\
\hline
{\em error\+\_\+out} & the buffer whether an error occurred during the individual calculation (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em handle\+\_\+content\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the first operand for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies whether the first operand is an interval value \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Min\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the minimum/lower interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum/upper interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Min\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the minimum/lower interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the maximum/upper interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves whether the result of the individual calculation is an interval value (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em number\+Of\+Trusted\+Digits\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum precision in digits for this individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em reference\+Pecision\+Cut\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum number of digits that are not trusted for this individual calculation \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

this interval function determines and, if necessary, returns the minimum/lower and maximum/upper interval limits of a mathematical modulo operation (like Python, e.\+g. (-\/1) mod 10 = 9) of two floating point numbers (like Python) with the specified precision (annotation\+: the following applies to the mathematical variant a mod b = ((a \% b) + b) \% b) 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em handle\+\_\+e\+Operator\+\_\+in} & specifies identifies the type of operator (e.\+g. ADDITION\+\_\+\+SIGN) for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em use\+Calculation\+Precision\+\_\+in} & specifies the precision for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em result\+\_\+in} & specifies the result of the standard calculation, i.\+e. without interval arithmetic \\
\hline
{\em error\+\_\+out} & the buffer whether an error occurred during the individual calculation (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em handle\+\_\+content\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the first operand for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em handle\+\_\+content\+Value\+Field2\+\_\+in} & specifies the possible second operand for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies whether the first operand is an interval value \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field2\+\_\+in} & specifies whether the possible second operand is an interval value \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Min\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the minimum/lower interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum/upper interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Min\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field2\+\_\+in} & specifies the minimum/lower interval limit of the possible second operand \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field2\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum/upper interval limit of the possible second operand \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Min\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the minimum/lower interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the maximum/upper interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves whether the result of the individual calculation is an interval value (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em number\+Of\+Trusted\+Digits\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum precision in digits for this individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em reference\+Pecision\+Cut\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum number of digits that are not trusted for this individual calculation \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

this interval function determines and, if necessary, returns the minimum/lower and maximum/upper interval limits of the normalize value function (e.\+g. norm(x)) with the specified precision 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em handle\+\_\+e\+Operator\+\_\+in} & specifies identifies the type of operator (e.\+g. ADDITION\+\_\+\+SIGN) for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em use\+Calculation\+Precision\+\_\+in} & specifies the precision for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em result\+\_\+in} & specifies the result of the standard calculation, i.\+e. without interval arithmetic \\
\hline

\hline

\hline

\hline

\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum/upper interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Min\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the minimum/lower interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the maximum/upper interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves whether the result of the individual calculation is an interval value (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em number\+Of\+Trusted\+Digits\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum precision in digits for this individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em reference\+Pecision\+Cut\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum number of digits that are not trusted for this individual calculation \\
\hline

{\em handle\+\_\+e\+Operator\+\_\+in} & specifies identifies the type of operator (e.\+g. ADDITION\+\_\+\+SIGN) for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em use\+Calculation\+Precision\+\_\+in} & specifies the precision for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em result\+\_\+in} & specifies the result of the standard calculation, i.\+e. without interval arithmetic \\
\hline
{\em error\+\_\+out} & the buffer whether an error occurred during the individual calculation (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em handle\+\_\+content\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the first operand for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies whether the first operand is an interval value \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Min\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the minimum/lower interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum/upper interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Min\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the minimum/lower interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the maximum/upper interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves whether the result of the individual calculation is an interval value (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em number\+Of\+Trusted\+Digits\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum precision in digits for this individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em reference\+Pecision\+Cut\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum number of digits that are not trusted for this individual calculation \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\em use\+Calculation\+Precision\+\_\+in} & specifies the precision for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em result\+\_\+in} & specifies the result of the standard calculation, i.\+e. without interval arithmetic \\
\hline
{\em error\+\_\+out} & the buffer whether an error occurred during the individual calculation (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em handle\+\_\+content\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the first operand for the individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies whether the first operand is an interval value \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Min\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the minimum/lower interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em stack\+Of\+Trusted\+Max\+Values\+\_\+handle\+\_\+\+Value\+Field1\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum/upper interval limit of the first operand \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Min\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the minimum/lower interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em trusted\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves the maximum/upper interval limit of the individual calculation (annotation\+: in case of an error the value is not specified) \\
\hline
{\em has\+Trusted\+Min\+Max\+Result\+\_\+in\+\_\+out} & this buffer retrieves whether the result of the individual calculation is an interval value (true) or not (false) \\
\hline
{\em number\+Of\+Trusted\+Digits\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum precision in digits for this individual calculation \\
\hline
{\em reference\+Pecision\+Cut\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum number of digits that are not trusted for this individual calculation \\

{\em reference\+Pecision\+Cut\+\_\+in} & specifies the maximum number of digits that are not trusted for this individual calculation \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
